{

 for (i = 0; i < number; ++i)

 printf("%d", (mass[gay - 1] - mass[gay - 2])); 
 getchar(); 
 getchar();

      Record* FindKey(Record* head,int i) 
{ 
 if (head->name[i] == 'A' || head->name[i] == 'a') 
 head->key = 1; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'B' || head->name[i] == 'b') 
 head->key = 2; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'C' || head->name[i] == 'c') 
 head->key = 3; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'D' || head->name[i] == 'd') 
 head->key = 4; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'E' || head->name[i] == 'e') 
 head->key = 5; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'F' || head->name[i] == 'f') 
 head->key = 6; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'G' || head->name[i] == 'g') 
 head->key = 7; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'H' || head->name[i] == 'ah') 
 head->key = 8; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'I' || head->name[i] == 'i') 
 head->key = 9; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'J' || head->name[i] == 'j') 
 head->key = 10; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'K' || head->name[i] == 'k') 
 head->key = 11; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'L' || head->name[i] == 'l') 
 head->key = 12; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'M' || head->name[i] == 'm') 
 head->key = 13; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'N' || head->name[i] == 'n') 
 head->key = 14; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'O' || head->name[i] == 'o') 
 head->key = 15; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'P' || head->name[i] == 'p') 
 head->key = 16; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'Q' || head->name[i] == 'q') 
 head->key = 17; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'R' || head->name[i] == 'r') 
 head->key = 18; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'S' || head->name[i] == 's') 
 head->key = 19; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'T' || head->name[i] == 't') 
 head->key = 20; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'U' || head->name[i] == 'u') 
 head->key = 21; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'V' || head->name[i] == 'v') 
 head->key = 22; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'W' || head->name[i] == 'w') 
 head->key = 23; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'X' || head->name[i] == 'x') 
 head->key = 24; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'Y' || head->name[i] == 'y') 
 head->key = 25; 
 else if (head->name[i] == 'Z' || head->name[i] == 'z') 
 head->key = 26; 
 if (head->next != NULL) 
 head->next = FindKey(head->next, i); 
 return head; 
}

app.use(session({ secret: 'keyboard cat', cookie: { maxAge: 60000 }}))

app.use(function(req, res, next) {
 var sess = req.session
 if (sess.views) {
 sess.views++
 res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'text/html')
 res.write('<p>views: ' + sess.views + '</p>')
 res.write('<p>expires in: ' + (sess.cookie.maxAge / 1000) + 's</p>')
 res.end()
 } else {
 sess.views = 1
 res.end('welcome to the session demo. refresh!')
 }
})

root@OpenWrt:/# cat /etc/profile
#!/bin/sh
[ -f /etc/banner ] && cat /etc/banner

export PATH=/bin:/sbin:/usr/bin:/usr/sbin
export HOME=$(grep -e "^${USER:-root}:" /etc/passwd | cut -d ":" -f 6)
export HOME=${HOME:-/root}
export PS1='\u@\h:\w\$ '

[ -x /bin/more ] || alias more=less
[ -x /usr/bin/vim ] && alias vi=vim || alias vim=vi

[ -z "$KSH_VERSION" -o \! -s /etc/mkshrc ] || . /etc/mkshrc

[ -x /usr/bin/arp ] || arp() { cat /proc/net/arp; }
[ -x /usr/bin/ldd ] || ldd() { LD_TRACE_LOADED_OBJECTS=1 $*; }
export PATH=<current default path>:/opt/bin:/opt/sbin:/opt/usr/bin:/opt/usr/sbin
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=<current default LD library path>:/opt/lib:/opt/usr/lib

ldconfig /mnt/sda4/usr/lib
ldconfig /mnt/sda4/lib
ldconfig /mnt/sda4/usr/lib
ldconfig /mnt/sda4/lib
export PATH=$PATH":/mnt/sda4/usr/bin"
